ISO date string\n    'country': 'str',\n    'age': 'float64',      # Allow NaN for missing\n    'is_active': 'bool'\n}\n\n# ------------------------------\n# Data Ingestion\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef ingest_raw_data(file_path: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Reads raw customer data from a CSV file.\n    \"\"\"\n    df = pd.read_csv(file_path)\n    print(f\"[Ingestion] Loaded {len(df)} rows from {file_path}\")\n    return df\n\n# ------------------------------\n# Data Cleaning & Transformation\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, str]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Cleans and transforms raw data to match the expected schema.\n    Handles missing columns, type conversions, and basic data quality.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Add missing columns with default values\n    for col, dtype in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if 'int' in dtype or 'float' in dtype:\n                df[col] = np.nan\n            elif dtype == 'bool':\n                df[col] = False\n            else:\n                df[col] = None\n            print(f\"[Schema] Added missing column: {col}\")\n\n    # Drop extra columns not in expected schema\n    extra_cols = set(df.columns) - set(expected_schema.keys())\n    if extra_cols:\n        print(f\"[Schema] Dropping extra columns: {extra_cols}\")\n        df = df.drop(columns=list(extra_cols))\n\n    # Enforce data types and clean data\n    for col, dtype in expected_schema.items():\n        if dtype == 'int64':\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').astype('Int64')\n        elif dtype == 'float64':\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce')\n        elif dtype == 'bool':\n            df[col] = df[col].astype('bool', errors='ignore')\n        elif dtype == 'str':\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).replace({'nan': None, 'NaT': None})\n        # Add more sophisticated cleaning as needed\n\n    # Data quality: remove rows with missing customer_id or email\n    before = len(df)\n    df = df.dropna(subset=['customer_id', 'email'])\n    after = len(df)\n    print(f\"[Quality] Dropped {before - after} rows with missing customer_id or email\")\n\n    # Standardize email\n    df['email'] = df['email'].str.lower().str.strip()\n\n    # Convert signup_date to ISO format\n    df['signup_date'] = pd.to_datetime(df['signup_date'], errors='coerce').dt.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n\n    return df\n\n# ------------------------------\n# Data Loading (Warehouse/Lake)\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table_name: str = \"customers\"):\n    \"\"\"\n    Loads cleaned data into a SQLite data warehouse, handling schema changes.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cursor = conn.cursor()\n\n    # Create table with dynamic schema\n    columns_with_types = []\n    for col, dtype in EXPECTED_SCHEMA.items():\n        if dtype == 'int64' or dtype == 'Int64':\n            col_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif dtype == 'float64':\n            col_type = 'REAL'\n        elif dtype == 'bool':\n            col_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        else:\n            col_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns_with_types.append(f\"{col} {col_type}\")\n\n    create_table_sql = f\"\"\"\n    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table_name} (\n        {', '.join(columns_with_types)}\n    );\n    \"\"\"\n    cursor.execute(create_table_sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\n    # Upsert data (replace existing customer_id)\n    for _, row in df.iterrows():\n        placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(EXPECTED_SCHEMA))\n        columns = ','.join(EXPECTED_SCHEMA.keys())\n        update_columns = ','.join([f\"{col}=excluded.{col}\" for col in EXPECTED_SCHEMA.keys() if col != 'customer_id'])\n        upsert_sql = f\"\"\"\n        INSERT INTO {table_name} ({columns})\n        VALUES ({placeholders})\n        ON CONFLICT(customer_id) DO UPDATE SET {update_columns};\n        \"\"\"\n        cursor.execute(upsert_sql, tuple(row[col] for col in EXPECTED_SCHEMA.keys()))\n    conn.commit()\n    print(f\"[Warehouse] Loaded {len(df)} rows into {table_name} table at {db_path}\")\n    conn.close()\n\n# ------------------------------\n# Semantic Layer Creation\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, output_path: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Creates a semantic layer view for AI-driven queries.\n    For demonstration, create an aggregated CSV with key features.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    query = \"\"\"\n    SELECT \n        country,\n        COUNT(*) AS customer_count,\n        AVG(age) AS avg_age,\n        SUM(CASE WHEN is_active THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS active_customers,\n        MIN(signup_date) AS first_signup,\n        MAX(signup_date) AS last_signup\n    FROM customers\n    GROUP BY country\n    ORDER BY customer_count DESC;\n    \"\"\"\n    df = pd.read_sql_query(query, conn)\n    df.to_csv(output_path, index=False)\n    print(f\"[Semantic Layer] Semantic view saved to {output_path}\")\n    conn.close()\n\n# ------------------------------\n# Main Pipeline\n# ------------------------------\n\ndef main():\n    #                         "\"\"\"\nData Ingestion and Transformation Pipeline for Customer Data\n\nThis script demonstrates a simplified end-to-end data pipeline:\n- Ingests raw customer data (CSV format) from a source directory.\n- Cleans and transforms the data (handles missing values, type coercion, deduplication).\n- Loads the processed data into a local SQLite \"data warehouse\".\n- Maintains a semantic layer (via a view) for AI-driven queries.\n- Handles schema changes and performs data quality checks.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport glob\nimport pandas as pd\nimport sqlite3\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any\n\n# ----------------- Configuration -----------------\nRAW_DATA_DIR = 'raw_data'\nWAREHOUSE_DB = 'customer_warehouse.db'\nTABLE_NAME = 'customers'\nSEMANTIC_VIEW = 'customer_semantic_view'\n\n# Define the expected schema for the customer data\nEXPECTED_SCHEMA = {\n    'customer_id': 'int',\n    'name': 'str',\n    'email': 'str',\n    'signup_date': 'datetime64[ns]',\n    'country': 'str',\n    'age': 'float',\n    'is_active': 'bool'\n}\n\n# Data quality rules\nREQUIRED_FIELDS = ['customer_id', 'email', 'signup_date']\n\n# -------------------------------------------------\n\ndef read_raw_data(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Read all CSV files from the raw data directory and concatenate them.\"\"\"\n    all_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(raw_dir, \"*.csv\"))\n    if not all_files:\n        raise FileNotFoundError(f\"No CSV files found in {raw_dir}\")\n    df_list = []\n    for file in all_files:\n        df = pd.read_csv(file)\n        df['__source_file'] = os.path.basename(file)  # Track source\n        df_list.append(df)\n    combined = pd.concat(df_list, ignore_index=True)\n    print(f\"[INFO] Loaded {len(combined)} records from {len(all_files)} files.\")\n    return combined\n\ndef align_schema(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, str]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Ensure DataFrame columns match the expected schema, adding missing columns as needed.\"\"\"\n    for col, dtype in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            print(f\"[WARN] Column '{col}' missing in raw data. Filling with NaN.\")\n            df[col] = pd.NA\n    # Drop unexpected columns\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys()) + ['__source_file']]\n    return df\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, str]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Clean and transform the data according to the expected schema.\"\"\"\n    # Type coercion and cleaning\n    for col, dtype in expected_schema.items():\n        if dtype == 'int':\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').astype('Int64')\n        elif dtype == 'float':\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce')\n        elif dtype == 'bool':\n            df[col] = df[col].astype('boolean')\n        elif dtype == 'datetime64[ns]':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n        else:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype('string')\n    # Deduplicate by customer_id, keeping the latest signup_date\n    df = df.sort_values('signup_date').drop_duplicates('customer_id', keep='last')\n    # Data quality: Remove rows missing required fields\n    before = len(df)\n    df = df.dropna(subset=REQUIRED_FIELDS)\n    after = len(df)\n    print(f\"[INFO] Dropped {before - after} rows failing data quality checks.\")\n    return df\n\ndef handle_schema_changes(conn: sqlite3.Connection, df: pd.DataFrame, table_name: str):\n    \"\"\"Alter the table to add any new columns found in the DataFrame.\"\"\"\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table_name})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col in df.columns:\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            dtype = infer_sqlite_type(df[col])\n            print(f\"[INFO] Adding new column '{col}' ({dtype}) to {table_name}.\")\n            cur.execute(f\"ALTER TABLE {table_name} ADD COLUMN {col} {dtype}\")\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef infer_sqlite_type(series: pd.Series) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Infer SQLite column type from pandas Series.\"\"\"\n    if pd.api.types.is_integer_dtype(series):\n        return \"INTEGER\"\n    elif pd.api.types.is_float_dtype(series):\n        return \"REAL\"\n    elif pd.api.types.is_bool_dtype(series):\n        return \"BOOLEAN\"\n    elif pd.api.types.is_datetime64_any_dtype(series):\n        return \"TIMESTAMP\"\n    else:\n        return \"TEXT\"\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table_name: str):\n    \"\"\"Load cleaned data into the SQLite data warehouse, handling schema changes.\"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    # Create table if it doesn't exist\n    columns_sql = ', '.join(f\"{col} {infer_sqlite_type(df[col])}\" for col in df.columns)\n    create_sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table_name} ({columns_sql})\"\n    conn.execute(create_sql)\n    # Handle schema changes (new columns)\n    handle_schema_changes(conn, df, table_name)\n    # Upsert data (replace by customer_id)\n    for _, row in df.iterrows():\n        placeholders = ', '.join(['?'] * len(df.columns))\n        columns = ', '.join(df.columns)\n        update_assignments = ', '.join([f\"{col}=excluded.{col}\" for col in df.columns if col != 'customer_id'])\n        sql = f\"\"\"\n            INSERT INTO {table_name} ({columns}) VALUES ({placeholders})\n            ON CONFLICT(customer_id) DO UPDATE SET {update_assignments}\n        \"\"\"\n        try:\n            conn.execute(sql, tuple(row))\n        except sqlite3.OperationalError as e:\n            print(f\"[ERROR] Failed to upsert row: {e}\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n    print(f\"[INFO] Loaded {len(df)} records into warehouse table '{table_name}'.\")\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, table_name: str, view_name: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create a semantic view for AI-driven queries.\n    This view can include business logic, calculated fields, or only expose selected columns.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    # Example: Expose only active customers with selected columns and calculated fields\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id,\n            name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            -- Example calculated field\n            CASE\n                WHEN age >= 18 THEN 'adult'\n                ELSE 'minor'\n            END AS age_group\n        FROM {table_name}\n        WHERE is_active = 1\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n    print(f\"[INFO] Created semantic view '{view_name}'.\")\n\ndef run_pipeline():\n    # Step 1: Ingest raw data\n    raw_df = read_raw_data(RAW_DATA_DIR)\n    # Step 2: Align schema (handle missing/new columns)\n    aligned_df = align_schema(raw_df, EXPECTED_SCHEMA)\n    # Step 3: Clean and transform\n    cleaned_df = clean_and_transform(aligned_df, EXPECTED_SCHEMA)\n    # Step 4: Load to warehouse\n    load_to_warehouse(cleaned_df, WAREHOUSE_DB, TABLE_NAME)\n    # Step 5: Create semantic layer\n    create_semantic_layer(WAREHOUSE_DB, TABLE_NAME, SEMANTIC_VIEW)\n    print(\"[INFO] Pipeline completed successfully.\")\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    # Ensure raw_data directory exists for demonstration\n    os.makedirs(RAW_DATA_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n    # Optionally: Place sample CSVs in RAW_DATA_DIR before running\n    run_pipeline()"

evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema):\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            cur.execute(f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\")\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema):\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(\"No raw data files found in directory.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\ndef col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    df.to_sql(table, conn, if_exists='append', index=False, method='multi')\n conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW                         "import unittest\nimport tempfile\nimport shutil\nimport os\nimport json\nimport pandas as pd\nimport sqlite3\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom pandas.testing import assert_frame_equal\n\n# Import functions from the code to test\n# (Assume code is in the same file for this test suite, otherwise use `from module import ...`)\n# Functions to test:\n# ingest_raw_files, clean_and_transform, evolve_schema, create_table_if_not_exists,\n# load_to_warehouse, create_semantic_layer\n\n# Copy-paste the EXPECTED_SCHEMA from the code\nEXPECTED_SCHEMA = {\n    'customer_id': str,\n    'first_name': str,\n    'last_name': str,\n    'email': str,\n    'signup_date': 'date',\n    'country': str,\n    'age': int,\n    'is_active': bool\n}\n\n# Copy-paste the functions to test (minimal, only for test suite to run)\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(\"No raw data files found in directory.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema):\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.lower().map({'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True}).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@')]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today())\n    return df\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema):\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            elif col_type == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            cur.execute(f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\")\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema):\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    df.to_sql(table, conn, if_exists='append', index=False, method='multi')\n    conn.execute(f\"\"\"\n        DELETE FROM {table}\n        WHERE rowid NOT IN (\n            SELECT MIN(rowid)\n            FROM {table}\n            GROUP BY customer_id\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            first_name || ' ' || last_name AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\nclass TestDataPipeline(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a temp directory for raw data files\n        self.test_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()\n        # Create a import ...\n\n# --- Begin code from user ---\n\nRAW_DATA_DIR = './raw_data'\nDATA_WAREHOUSE_DB = './data_warehouse.db'\nSEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW = 'customer_semantic_view'\n\nEXPECTED_SCHEMA = {\n    'customer_id': str,\n    'first_name': str,\n    'last_name': str,\n    'email': str,\n    'signup_date': 'date',\n    'country': str,\n    'age': int,\n    'is_active': bool\n}\n\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(\"No raw data files found in directory.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema):\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.lower().map({'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True}).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@')]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today())\n    return df\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema):\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            elif col_type == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            cur.execute(f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\")\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema):\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    df.to_sql(table, conn, if_exists='append', index=False, method='multi')\n    conn.execute(f\"\"\"\n        DELETE FROM {table}\n        WHERE rowid NOT IN (\n            SELECT MIN(rowid)\n            FROM {table}\n            GROUP BY customer_id\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            first_name || ' ' || last_name AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\n# --- End code from user ---\n\nclass TestCustomerDataPipeline(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Setup a temporary directory for raw 'customer_semantic_view'\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        shutil.rmtree(self.test_dir)\n        os.close(self.db_fd)\n        os.remove(self.db_path)\n\n    def write_json(self, filename, data):\n df.to_csv(os.path.join(self.test_dir, filename), index=False)\n\n    def test_ingest_json_and_csv(self):\n        # JSON file\n        json_data = [\n            {\n                \"customer_id\": \"C1\",\n                \"first_name\": \"Alice\",\n                \"last_name\": \"Smith\",\n                \"email\": \"alice@example.com\",\n                \"signup_date\": \"2023-01-01\",\n                \"country\": \"US\",\n                \"age\": 30,\n                \"is_active\": True\n            }\n        ]\n        self.write_json('data1.json', json_data)\n        # CSV file\n        df_csv = pd.DataFrame([\n            {\n                \"customer_id\": \"C2\",\n                \"first_name\": \"Bob\",\n                \"last_name\": \"Brown\",\n                \"email\": \"bob@example.com\",\n                \"signup_date\": \"2022-12-31\",\n                \"country\": \"UK\",\n                \"age\": 25,\n                \"is_active\": False\n            }\n        ])\n        self.write_csv('data2.csv', df_csv)\n        df = ingest_raw_files(self.test_dir)\n        self.assertEqual(len(df), 2)\n        self.assertIn('customer_id', df.columns)\n        self.assertIn('email', df.columns)\n        self.assertSetEqual(set(df['customer_id']), {'C1', 'C2'})\n\n    def test_ingest_no_files(self):\n        # Directory is empty\n        with self.assertRaises(ValueError):\n            ingest_raw_files(self.test_dir)\n\n    def test_clean_and_transform_missing_columns(self):\n        # Only customer_id and email provided; others missing\n clean_and_transform(df, EXPECTED_SCHEMA)\n        self.assertEqual(set(clean_df.columns), set(EXPECTED_SCHEMA.keys()))\n        self.assertTrue((clean_df['first_name'] == 'Unknown').all())\n        self.assertTrue((clean_df['last_name'] == 'Unknown').all())\n        self.assertTrue((clean_df['age'] == 0).all())\n        self.assertTrue((clean_df['is_active'] == False).all())\n        self.assertTrue((clean_df['country'] == '').all())\n        self.assertTrue(pd.api.types.is_datetime64_any_dtype(clean_df['signup_date']))\n\n    def test_clean_and_transform_type_conversion(self):\n warehouse\nSEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW = 'customer_semantic_view'\n\n# Define expected schema and types for customer data\nEXPECTED_SCHEMA = {\n    'customer_id': str,\n    'first_name': str,\n    'last_name': str,\n    'email': str,\n    'signup_date': 'date',    # Custom type for date\n    'country': str,\n    'age': int,\n    'is_active': bool\n}\n\n# -------------------- DATA INGESTION --------------------\n\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Ingest raw customer data from JSON and CSV files in the specified directory.\n    Returns a concatenated DataFrame.\n    \"\"\"\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(\"No raw data files found in directory.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\n# -------------------- DATA QUALITY & TRANSFORMATION --------------------\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Clean and transform raw DataFrame according to the expected schema.\n    Handles missing columns, type conversion, and basic data quality checks.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Add missing columns with default values\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    \n    # Remove extra columns\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    \n    # Type conversions and cleaning\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.lower().map({'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True}).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    \n    # Data quality checks\n    # Remove rows without customer_id or email\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@')]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    \n    # Fill missing names with 'Unknown'\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    \n    # Ensure age is within reasonable bounds\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    \n    # Fill missing signup_date with today's date\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today())\n    \n    return df\n\n# -------------------- SCHEMA EVOLUTION HANDLING --------------------\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ensure the warehouse table matches the expected schema.\n    Adds missing columns as needed.\n    \"\"\"\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            elif col_type == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            cur.execute(f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\")\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create the warehouse table if it does not exist.\n    \"\"\"\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\n# -------------------- LOAD TO DATA WAREHOUSE --------------------\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Load cleaned DataFrame into the warehouse, handling schema evolution.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    # Upsert logic: replace existing rows with same customer_id\n    df.to_sql(table, conn, if_exists='append', index=False, method='multi')\n    # Remove duplicates (keep latest)\n    conn.execute(f\"\"\"\n        DELETE FROM {table}\n        WHERE rowid NOT IN (\n            SELECT MIN(rowid)\n            FROM {table}\n            GROUP BY customer_id\n        )\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- SEMANTIC LAYER CREATION --------------------\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create a semantic view for AI-driven queries.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    # Example: create a view with derived columns and friendly names\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            first_name || ' ' || last_name AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- MAIN PIPELINE --------------------\n\ndef main():\n    print(\"Starting data pipeline...\")\n    # 1. Ingest raw data\n    print(\"Ingesting raw data...\")\n    raw_df = ingest_raw_files(RAW_DATA_DIR)\n    # 2. Clean and transform\n    print(\"Cleaning and transforming data...\")\n    clean_df = clean_and_transform(raw_df, EXPECTED_SCHEMA)\n    # 3. Load into data warehouse\n    print(\"Loading data into warehouse...\")\n    load_to_warehouse(clean_df, DATA_WAREHOUSE_DB, 'customers', EXPECTED_SCHEMA)\n    # 4. Create semantic layer\n    print(\"Creating semantic layer...\")\n    create_semantic_layer(DATA_WAREHOUSE_DB, 'customers', SEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW)\n    print(\"Pipeline completed successfully.\")\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    main()",

DataFrame.\n    \"\"\"\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, [records]\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n TRANSFORMATION --------------------\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Clean and transform raw DataFrame according to the expected schema.\n    Handles missing columns, type conversion, and basic data quality checks.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Add missing columns with default values\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    \n    # Remove extra columns\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    \n    # {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            alter_sql = f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\"\n            cur.execute(alter_sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create the warehouse table if it does not exist.\n    \"\"\"\n elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\n# -------------------- LOAD TO DATA WAREHOUSE --------------------\n\ndef upsert_customers(conn: sqlite3.Connection, df: pd.DataFrame, table: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Upsert (insert or replace) customer records into the warehouse table.\n    Uses SQLite's INSERT OR REPLACE for idempotency.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Prepare columns and values\n    cols = list(df.columns)\n    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(cols))\n    col_names = ','.join(cols)\n    sql = f\"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table} ({col_names}) VALUES ({placeholders})\"\n    values = [tuple(row) for row in df.itertuples(index=False, DataFrame into the warehouse, handling schema evolution and upserts.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n conn.cursor()\n    # Drop existing view if it exists\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    # Create new view with derived columns and friendly names\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, primary_key: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Upsert records into SQLite table using INSERT OR REPLACE.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Prepare columns and placeholders\n    cols = df.columns.tolist()\n    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(cols))\n    insert_sql = f\"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table} ({','.join(cols)}) VALUES ({placeholders})\"\n    data = [tuple(row) for row in df.itertuples(index=False, name=None)]\n    conn.executemany(insert_sql, data)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Load cleaned DataFrame into the warehouse, handling schema evolution and upsert.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path, detect_types=sqlite3.PARSE_DECLTYPES | sqlite3.PARSE_COLNAMES)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    # Convert datetime to string for SQLite DATE columns\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = df[col].dt.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n    upsert_to_sqlite(df, conn, table, primary_key='customer_id')\n semantic view with derived columns and friendly names\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            first_name || ' ' || last_name AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- MAIN PIPELINE --------------------\n\ndef main():\n    print(\"Starting data pipeline...\")\n    # 1. Ingest raw data\n    print(\"Ingesting raw data...\")\n    raw_df = ingest_raw_files(RAW_DATA_DIR)\n    # 2.                         "import os\nimport json\nimport sqlite3\nimport pandas as pd\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import Dict, Any\n\n# -------------------- CONFIGURATION --------------------\n\nRAW_DATA_DIR = './raw_data'                    # Directory containing raw JSON/CSV files\nDATA_WAREHOUSE_DB = './data_warehouse.db'      # SQLite DB file for data warehouse\nWAREHOUSE_TABLE = 'customers'\nSEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW = 'customer_semantic_view'\n\n# Define expected schema and types for customer data\nEXPECTED_SCHEMA = {\n    'customer_id': str,\n    'first_name': str,\n    'last_name': str,\n    'email': str,\n    'signup_date': 'date',    # Custom type for date\n    'country': str,\n    'age': int,\n    'is_active': bool\n}\n\n# -------------------- DATA INGESTION --------------------\n\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Ingest raw customer data from JSON and CSV files in the specified directory.\n    Returns a concatenated DataFrame.\n    \"\"\"\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            # Support both list of dicts and dict (single record)\n            if isinstance(records, dict):\n                records = [records]\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(\"No raw data files found in directory.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\n# -------------------- DATA QUALITY & TRANSFORMATION --------------------\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Clean and transform raw DataFrame according to the expected schema.\n    Handles missing columns, type conversion, and basic data quality checks.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Add missing columns with default values\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    \n    # Remove extra columns\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    \n    # Type conversions and cleaning\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            # Accept various representations of boolean\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.strip().str.lower().map({'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True, 'false': False, '0': False, 'no': False}).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    \n    # Data quality checks\n    # Remove rows without customer_id or email\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@', na=False)]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    \n    # Fill missing names with 'Unknown'\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    \n    # Ensure age is within reasonable bounds\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    \n    # Fill missing signup_date with today's date\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today().normalize())\n    \n    # Ensure country is not missing\n    df['country'] = df['country'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    \n    return df\n\n# -------------------- SCHEMA EVOLUTION HANDLING --------------------\n\ndef get_sql_type(col_type):\n    \"\"\"\n    Map Python type or custom type to SQLite type.\n    \"\"\"\n    if col_type == str:\n        return 'TEXT'\n    elif col_type == int:\n        return 'INTEGER'\n    elif col_type == bool:\n        return 'BOOLEAN'\n    elif col_type == 'date':\n        return 'DATE'\n    else:\n        return 'TEXT'\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create the warehouse table if it does not exist.\n    \"\"\"\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        sql_type = get_sql_type(col_type)\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ensure the warehouse table matches the expected schema.\n    Adds missing columns as needed.\n    \"\"\"\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            sql_type = get_sql_type(col_type)\n            cur.execute(f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\")\n    conn.commit()\n\n# -------------------- LOAD TO DATA WAREHOUSE --------------------\n\ndef upsert_to_sqlite(df: pd.DataFrame, conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, pk_col: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Upsert rows into SQLite table based on primary key.\n    Uses INSERT OR REPLACE for efficiency.\n    \"\"\"\n    cols = list(df.columns)\n    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(cols))\n    col_names = ','.join(cols)\n    sql = f\"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table} ({col_names}) VALUES ({placeholders})\"\n    data = [tuple(row) for row in df[cols].itertuples(index=False, name=None)]\n    with conn:\n        conn.executemany(sql, data)\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Load cleaned DataFrame into the warehouse, handling schema evolution and upsert.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    upsert_to_sqlite(df, conn, table, pk_col='customer_id')\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- SEMANTIC LAYER CREATION --------------------\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create a semantic view for AI-driven queries.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    # Drop existing view if present\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    # Create semantic view with derived columns and friendly names\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            TRIM(first_name) || ' ' || TRIM(last_name) AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- MAIN PIPELINE --------------------\n\ndef main():\n    print(\"Starting data pipeline...\")\n    # 1. Ingest raw data\n    print(\"Ingesting raw data...\")\n    raw_df = ingest_raw_files(RAW_DATA_DIR)\n    # 2. Clean and transform\n    print(\"Cleaning and transforming data...\")\n    clean_df = clean_and_transform(raw_df, EXPECTED_SCHEMA)\n    # 3. Load into data warehouse\n    print(\"Loading data into warehouse...\")\n    load_to_warehouse(clean_df, DATA_WAREHOUSE_DB, WAREHOUSE_TABLE, EXPECTED_SCHEMA)\n    # 4. Create semantic layer\n    print(\"Creating semantic layer...\")\n    create_semantic_layer(DATA_WAREHOUSE_DB, WAREHOUSE_TABLE, SEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW)\n    print(\"Pipeline completed successfully.\")\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    main()"

                        "import os\nimport shutil\nimport tempfile\nimport unittest\nimport sqlite3\nimport json\nimport pandas as pd\nfrom datetime import datetime, date\n\n# Import the code to test (assume it's in the same file for this test suite)\n# If the code is in another module, you would do: from my_module import ...\n# For this test, we redefine the functions here as they're in the same file.\n\n# --- Begin of code under test (copy-pasted for context, but in practice, import) ---\nimport os\nimport json\nimport sqlite3\nimport pandas as pd\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, List\n\nRAW_DATA_DIR = './raw_data'\nDATA_WAREHOUSE_DB = './data_warehouse.db'\nWAREHOUSE_TABLE = 'customers'\nSEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW = 'customer_semantic_view'\n\nEXPECTED_SCHEMA = {\n    'customer_id': str,\n    'first_name': str,\n    'last_name': str,\n    'email': str,\n    'signup_date': 'date',\n    'country': str,\n    'age': int,\n    'is_active': bool\n}\n\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            if isinstance(records, dict):\n                records = [records]\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(f\"No raw data files found in directory {raw_dir}.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.strip().str.lower().map(\n                {'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True, 'false': False, '0': False, 'no': False}\n            ).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@', na=False)]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today().normalize())\n    return df\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            elif col_type == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            alter_sql = f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\"\n            cur.execute(alter_sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef upsert_customers(conn: sqlite3.Connection, df: pd.DataFrame, table: str):\n    cols = list(df.columns)\n    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(cols))\n    col_names = ','.join(cols)\n    sql = f\"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table} ({col_names}) VALUES ({placeholders})\"\n    values = [tuple(row) for row in df.itertuples(index=False, name=None)]\n    with conn:\n        conn.executemany(sql, values)\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    upsert_customers(conn, df, table)\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            first_name || ' ' || last_name AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n# --- End of code under test ---\n\nclass TestDataPipeline(unittest.TestCase):\n    def                         "import os\nimport shutil\nimport tempfile\nimport unittest\nimport json\nimport sqlite3\nimport pandas as pd\nfrom datetime import datetime, date\nfrom typing import Dict, Any\n\n# Import functions from the provided code\n# For this test suite, we assume the code to test is in the same file.\n# If it were in another module, e.g., pipeline.py, you'd use:\n# from pipeline import ingest_raw_files, clean_and_transform, ...\n\n# --- Begin: Copy-paste of the code under test (excluding main()) ---\n\nRAW_DATA_DIR = './raw_data'  # Directory containing raw JSON/CSV files\nDATA_WAREHOUSE_DB = './data_warehouse.db'  # SQLite DB file for data warehouse\nWAREHOUSE_TABLE = 'customers'\nSEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW = 'customer_semantic_view'\n\nEXPECTED_SCHEMA = {\n    'customer_id': str,\n    'first_name': str,\n    'last_name': str,\n    'email': str,\n    'signup_date': 'date',\n    'country': str,\n    'age': int,\n    'is_active': bool\n}\n\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            if isinstance(records, dict):\n                records = [records]\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(f\"No raw data files found in directory {raw_dir}.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.strip().str.lower().map(\n                {'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True, 'false': False, '0': False, 'no': False}\n            ).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@', na=False)]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today().normalize())\n    return df\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            elif col_type == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            alter_sql = f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\"\n            cur.execute(alter_sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef upsert_customers(conn: sqlite3.Connection, df: pd.DataFrame, table: str):\n    cols = list(df.columns)\n    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(cols))\n    col_names = ','.join(cols)\n    sql = f\"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table} ({col_names}) VALUES ({placeholders})\"\n    values = [tuple(row) for row in df.itertuples(index=False, name=None)]\n    with conn:\n        conn.executemany(sql, values)\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    upsert_customers(conn, df, table)\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            first_name || ' ' || last_name AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\n# --- End: Copy-paste of the code under test ---\n\nclass TestDataPipeline(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a temporary directory for raw data files\n        self.tempdir = tempfile.mkdtemp()\n        # Create a temporary SQLite database\n        self.db_fd, self.db_path = tempfile.mkstemp(suffix='.db')\n        self.table = 'customers'\n        self.view = 'customer_semantic_view'\n        self.schema = EXPECTED_SCHEMA\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        shutil.rmtree(self.tempdir)\n        os.close(self.db_fd)\n        os.remove(self.db_path)\n\n    def write_json(self, filename, data):\n        with open(os.path.join(self.tempdir, filename), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            json.dump(data, f)\n\n    def write_csv(self, filename, data, columns):\n        df = pd.DataFrame(data, columns=columns)\n        df.to_csv(os.path.join(self.tempdir, filename), index=False)\n\n    def test_ingest_json_and_csv(self):\n        # Write JSON file\n        self.write_json('customers1.json', [\n            {\"customer_id\": \"1\", \"first_name\": \"Alice\", \"last_name\": \"Smith\", \"email\": \"alice@ex.com\", \"signup_date\": \"2020-01-01\", \"country\": \"US\", \"age\": 30, \"is_active\": True}\n        ])\n        # Write CSV file\n        self.write_csv('customers2.csv', [\n            [\"2\", \"Bob\", \"Brown\", \"bob@ex.com\", \"2021-02-02\", \"UK\", 25, False]\n        ], columns=list(EXPECTED_SCHEMA.keys()))\n        df = ingest_raw_files(self.tempdir)\n        self.assertEqual(len(df), 2)\n        self.assertIn('customer_id', df.columns)\n        self.assertIn('email', df.columns)\n        # Check that both records are present\n        self.assertSetEqual(set(df['customer_id']), {'1', '2'})\n\n    def test_ingest_empty_dir(self):\n        # Directory is empty\n        with self.assertRaises(ValueError):\n            ingest_raw_files(self.tempdir)\n\n    def test_clean_and_transform_basic(self):\n        # Data with missing columns and wrong types\n        df = pd.DataFrame([\n            {\"customer_id\": \"1\", \"email\": \"alice@ex.com\", \"age\": \"notanumber\"},\n            {\"customer_id\": \"2\", \"email\": \"bobatex.com\", \"age\": 150, \"is_active\": \"yes\"},\n            {\"customer_id\": \"\", \"email\": \"noid@ex.com\", \"age\": 10},\n            {\"customer_id\": \"3\", \"email\": \"carol@ex.com\", \"first_name\": \"\", \"last_name\": \"\", \"age\": 17, \"is_active\": \"maybe\"},\n            {\"customer_id\": \"1\", \"email\": \"alice@ex.com\", \"age\": 35}  # Duplicate ID\n        ])\n        clean_df = clean_and_transform(df, EXPECTED_SCHEMA)\n        # Should drop duplicate and invalid email, and missing id\n        self.assertTrue(all(clean_df['email'].str.contains('@')))\n        self.assertNotIn('', clean_df['customer_id'].values)\n        self.assertEqual(len(clean_df), 2)  # Only unique valid IDs: '1' and '3'\n        # Names filled as 'Unknown'\n        self.assertTrue(all(clean_df['first_name'].notnull()))\n        self.assertIn('Unknown', clean_df['first_name'].values)\n        # Age out of bounds set to 0\n        self.assertTrue(all((clean_df['age'] >= 0) & (clean_df['age'] <= 120)))\n        # is_active defaulted to False if not valid\n        self.assertIn(False, clean_df['is_active'].values)\n        # signup_date filled\n        self.assertTrue(pd.notnull(clean_df['signup_date']).all())\n\n    def test_clean_and_transform_types(self):\n        # Test bool and date parsing\n        df = --------------------\n\nRAW_DATA_DIR = './raw_data'  # Directory containing raw JSON/CSV files\nDATA_WAREHOUSE_DB = './data_warehouse.db'  # SQLite DB file for data warehouse\nWAREHOUSE_TABLE = 'last_name': str,\n    'email': str,\n    'signup_date': 'date',    # Custom type for date\n    'country': str,\n    'age': int,\n    'is_active': bool\n}\n\n# -------------------- DATA INGESTION --------------------\n\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Ingest raw customer data from JSON and CSV files in the specified directory.\n    Returns a concatenated DataFrame.\n    \"\"\"\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            # Support both list of dicts and single dict\n            if isinstance(records, dict):\n                records = [records]\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(f\"No raw data files found in directory {raw_dir}.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\n# -------------------- DATA QUALITY & TRANSFORMATION --------------------\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Clean and transform raw DataFrame according to the expected schema.\n    Handles missing columns, type conversion, and basic data quality checks.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Add missing columns with default values\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    \n    # Remove extra columns\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    \n    # Type conversions and cleaning\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            # Accept various representations of boolean\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.strip().str.lower().map(\n                {'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True, 'false': False, '0': False, 'no': False}\n            ).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    \n    # Data quality checks\n    # Remove rows without customer_id or email\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@', na=False)]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    \n    # Fill missing names with 'Unknown'\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    \n    # Ensure age is within reasonable bounds\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    \n    # Fill missing signup_date with today's date\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today().normalize())\n    \n    return df\n\n# -------------------- SCHEMA EVOLUTION HANDLING --------------------\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ensure the warehouse table matches the expected schema.\n    Adds missing columns as needed.\n    \"\"\"\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            elif col_type == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            alter_sql = f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\"\n            cur.execute(alter_sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create the warehouse table if it does not exist.\n    \"\"\"\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\n# -------------------- LOAD TO DATA WAREHOUSE --------------------\n\ndef upsert_customers(conn: sqlite3.Connection, df: pd.DataFrame, table: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Upsert (insert or replace) customer records into the warehouse table.\n    Uses SQLite's INSERT OR REPLACE for idempotency.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Prepare columns and values\n    cols = list(df.columns)\n    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(cols))\n    col_names = ','.join(cols)\n    sql = f\"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table} ({col_names}) VALUES ({placeholders})\"\n    values = [tuple(row) for row in df.itertuples(index=False, name=None)]\n    with conn:\n        conn.executemany(sql, values)\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Load cleaned DataFrame into the warehouse, handling schema evolution and upserts.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    upsert_customers(conn, df, table)\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- SEMANTIC LAYER CREATION --------------------\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create a semantic view for AI-driven queries.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    # Drop existing view if it exists\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    # Create new view with derived columns and friendly names\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            first_name || ' ' || last_name AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- MAIN PIPELINE --------------------\n\ndef main():\n    print(\"Starting data pipeline...\")\n\n    # 1. Ingest raw data\n    print(\"Ingesting raw data...\")\n    raw_df = ingest_raw_files(RAW_DATA_DIR)\n    print(f\"Ingested {len(raw_df)} raw records.\")\n\n    # 2. Clean and transform\n    print(\"Cleaning and transforming data...\")\n    clean_df = clean_and_transform(raw_df, EXPECTED_SCHEMA)\n    print(f\"Cleaned dataset contains {len(clean_df)} records.\")\n\n    # 3. Load into data warehouse\n    print(\"Loading data into warehouse...\")\n    load_to_warehouse(clean_df, DATA_WAREHOUSE_DB, WAREHOUSE_TABLE, EXPECTED_SCHEMA)\n    print(\"Data loaded to warehouse.\")\n\n    # 4. Create semantic layer\n    print(\"Creating semantic layer (view)...\")\n    create_semantic_layer(DATA_WAREHOUSE_DB, WAREHOUSE_TABLE, SEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW)\n    print(f\"Semantic layer '{SEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW}' created.\")\n\n    print(\"Pipeline completed successfully.\")\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    main()",

                        "import os\nimport json\nimport sqlite3\nimport pandas as pd\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import Dict, Any\n\n# -------------------- CONFIGURATION --------------------\n\nRAW_DATA_DIR = './raw_data'  # Directory containing raw JSON/CSV files\nDATA_WAREHOUSE_DB = './data_warehouse.db'  # SQLite DB file for data warehouse\nWAREHOUSE_TABLE =
