'last_name': str,\n    'email': str,\n    'signup_date': 'date',    # Custom type for date\n    'country': str,\n    'age': int,\n    'is_active': bool\n}\n\n# -------------------- DATA INGESTION --------------------\n\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Ingest raw customer data from JSON and CSV files in the specified directory.\n    Returns a concatenated DataFrame.\n    \"\"\"\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            # Support both list of dicts and single dict\n            if isinstance(records, dict):\n                records = [records]\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(f\"No raw data files found in directory {raw_dir}.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\n# -------------------- DATA QUALITY & TRANSFORMATION --------------------\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Clean and transform raw DataFrame according to the expected schema.\n    Handles missing columns, type conversion, and basic data quality checks.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Add missing columns with default values\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    \n    # Remove extra columns\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    \n    # Type conversions and cleaning\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            # Accept various representations of boolean\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.strip().str.lower().map(\n                {'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True, 'false': False, '0': False, 'no': False}\n            ).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    \n    # Data quality checks\n    # Remove rows without customer_id or email\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@', na=False)]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    \n    # Fill missing names with 'Unknown'\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    \n    # Ensure age is within reasonable bounds\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    \n    # Fill missing signup_date with today's date\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today().normalize())\n    \n    return df\n\n# -------------------- SCHEMA EVOLUTION HANDLING --------------------\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ensure the warehouse table matches the expected schema.\n    Adds missing columns as needed.\n    \"\"\"\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            elif col_type == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            alter_sql = f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\"\n            cur.execute(alter_sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create the warehouse table if it does not exist.\n    \"\"\"\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\n# -------------------- LOAD TO DATA WAREHOUSE --------------------\n\ndef upsert_customers(conn: sqlite3.Connection, df: pd.DataFrame, table: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Upsert (insert or replace) customer records into the warehouse table.\n    Uses SQLite's INSERT OR REPLACE for idempotency.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Prepare columns and values\n    cols = list(df.columns)\n    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(cols))\n    col_names = ','.join(cols)\n    sql = f\"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table} ({col_names}) VALUES ({placeholders})\"\n    # Convert datetime columns to string for SQLite\n    values = []\n    for row in df.itertuples(index=False, name=None):\n        row = list(row)\n        for idx, col in enumerate(cols):\n            if EXPECTED_SCHEMA[col] == 'date':\n                if pd.isnull(row[idx]):\n                    row[idx] = None\n                elif isinstance(row[idx], pd.Timestamp):\n                    row[idx] = row[idx].strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n        values.append(tuple(row))\n    with conn:\n        conn.executemany(sql, values)\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Load cleaned DataFrame into the warehouse, handling schema evolution and upserts.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    upsert_customers(conn, df, table)\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- SEMANTIC LAYER CREATION --------------------\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create a semantic view for AI-driven queries.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    # Drop existing view if it exists\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    # Create new view with derived columns and friendly names\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            first_name || ' ' || last_name AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- MAIN PIPELINE 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n\n    # Data quality checks\n    # Remove rows without customer_id or email\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@', na=False)]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n\n    # Fill missing names with 'Unknown'\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n\n    # Ensure age is within reasonable bounds\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n\n    # Fill missing signup_date with today's date\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today().normalize())\n\n    return df\n\n# -------------------- SCHEMA EVOLUTION HANDLING --------------------\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ensure the warehouse table matches the expected schema.\n    Adds missing columns as needed.\n    \"\"\"\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            elif col_type == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            alter_sql = f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\"\n            cur.execute(alter_sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create the warehouse table if it does not exist.\n    \"\"\"\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\n# -------------------- LOAD TO DATA WAREHOUSE --------------------\n\ndef upsert_customers(conn: sqlite3.Connection, df: pd.DataFrame, table: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Upsert (insert or replace) customer records into the warehouse table.\n    Uses SQLite's INSERT OR REPLACE for idempotency.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Prepare columns and values\n    cols = list(df.columns)\n    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(cols))\n    col_names = ','.join(cols)\n    sql = f\"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table} ({col_names}) VALUES ({placeholders})\"\n    # Convert dates to string for SQLite compatibility\n    values = []\n    for row in df.itertuples(index=False, name=None):\n        row = list(row)\n        for idx, col in enumerate(cols):\n            if EXPECTED_SCHEMA[col] == 'date':\n                # Store as ISO string\n                if pd.isnull(row[idx]):\n                    row[idx] = None\n                else:\n                    row[idx] = pd.Timestamp(row[idx]).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n        values.append(tuple(row))\n    with conn:\n        conn.executemany(sql, values)\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Load cleaned DataFrame into the warehouse, handling schema evolution and upserts.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    upsert_customers(conn, df, table)\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- SEMANTIC LAYER CREATION --------------------\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create a semantic view for AI-driven queries.\n    \"\"\"\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    # Drop existing view if it exists\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    # Create new view with derived columns and friendly names\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            first_name || ' ' || last_name AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- MAIN PIPELINE                         "import os\nimport shutil\nimport tempfile\nimport unittest\nimport sqlite3\nimport pandas as pd\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\n\n# Import the functions to test from the provided code.\n# For this test, we assume the code above is in the same file or imported as a module.\n# If in another file, e.g., pipeline.py, you would use:\n# from provided implementation ----\nimport os\nimport json\nimport sqlite3\nimport pandas as pd\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import Dict, Any\n\nRAW_DATA_DIR = './raw_data'\nDATA_WAREHOUSE_DB = './data_warehouse.db'\nWAREHOUSE_TABLE = 'customers'\nSEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW = 'customer_semantic_view'\n\nEXPECTED_SCHEMA = {\n    'customer_id': str,\n    'first_name': str,\n    'last_name': str,\n    'email': str,\n    'signup_date': 'date',\n    'country': str,\n    'age': int,\n    'is_active': bool\n}\n\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            if isinstance(records, dict):\n                records = [records]\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(f\"No raw data files found in directory {raw_dir}.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.strip().str.lower().map(\n                {'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True, 'false': False, '0': False, 'no': False}\n            ).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@', na=False)]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today().normalize())\n    return df\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            elif col_type == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            alter_sql = f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\"\n            cur.execute(alter_sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef upsert_customers(conn: sqlite3.Connection, df: pd.DataFrame, table: str):\n    cols = list(df.columns)\n    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(cols))\n    col_names = ','.join(cols)\n    sql = f\"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO {table} ({col_names}) VALUES ({placeholders})\"\n    values = []\n    for row in df.itertuples(index=False, name=None):\n        row = list(row)\n        for idx, col in enumerate(cols):\n            if EXPECTED_SCHEMA[col] == 'date':\n                if pd.isnull(row[idx]):\n                    row[idx] = None\n                elif isinstance(row[idx], pd.Timestamp):\n                    row[idx] = row[idx].strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n        values.append(tuple(row))\n    with conn:\n        conn.executemany(sql, values)\n\ndef load_to_warehouse(df: pd.DataFrame, db_path: str, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    create_table_if_not_exists(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    evolve_schema(conn, table, expected_schema)\n    upsert_customers(conn, df, table)\n    conn.close()\n\ndef create_semantic_layer(db_path: str, base_table: str, view_name: str):\n    conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path)\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n        CREATE VIEW {view_name} AS\n        SELECT\n            customer_id AS id,\n            first_name || ' ' || last_name AS full_name,\n            email,\n            country,\n            age,\n            is_active,\n            signup_date,\n            CASE\n                WHEN age < 18 THEN 'Minor'\n                WHEN age BETWEEN 18 AND 64 THEN 'Adult'\n                ELSE 'Senior'\n            END AS age_group,\n            strftime('%Y', signup_date) AS signup_year\n        FROM {base_table}\n    \"\"\")\n    conn.commit()\n    conn.close()\n# ---- End pasted code ----\n\nclass                         "import os\nimport shutil\nimport tempfile\nimport unittest\nimport sqlite3\nimport json\nimport pandas as pd\nfrom datetime import datetime, date\nfrom typing import Dict, Any\n\n# Import the functions and constants from the code to test\n# (Assume the code is in the same script or adjust the import as necessary)\n# For this test, we redefine the constants and import functions directly.\n\n# -------------------- Begin: Copy of constants and functions --------------------\nRAW_DATA_DIR = './raw_data'\nDATA_WAREHOUSE_DB = './data_warehouse.db'\nWAREHOUSE_TABLE = 'customers'\nSEMANTIC_LAYER_VIEW = 'customer_semantic_view'\n\nEXPECTED_SCHEMA = {\n    'customer_id': str,\n    'first_name': str,\n    'last_name': str,\n    'email': str,\n    'signup_date': 'date',\n    'country': str,\n    'age': int,\n    'is_active': bool\n}\n\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            if isinstance(records, dict):\n                records = [records]\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(f\"No raw data files found in directory {raw_dir}.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.strip().str.lower().map(\n                {'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True, 'false': False, '0': False, 'no': False}\n            ).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@', na=False)]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today().normalize())\n    return df\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = {row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()}\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in existing_cols:\n            if col_type == str:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            elif col_type == int:\n                sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n            elif col_type == bool:\n                sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            alter_sql = f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\"\n            cur.execute(alter_sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY --------------------\n\ndef ingest_raw_files(raw_dir: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Ingest raw customer data from JSON and CSV files in the specified directory.\n    Returns a concatenated DataFrame.\n    \"\"\"\n    all_dfs = []\n    for fname in os.listdir(raw_dir):\n        fpath = os.path.join(raw_dir, fname)\n        if fname.lower().endswith('.json'):\n            with open(fpath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                records = json.load(f)\n            # Support both list of dicts and single dict\n            if isinstance(records, dict):\n                records = [records]\n            df = pd.DataFrame(records)\n        elif fname.lower().endswith('.csv'):\n            df = pd.read_csv(fpath)\n        else:\n            continue\n        all_dfs.append(df)\n    if not all_dfs:\n        raise ValueError(f\"No raw data files found in directory {raw_dir}.\")\n    return pd.concat(all_dfs, ignore_index=True)\n\n# -------------------- DATA QUALITY & TRANSFORMATION --------------------\n\ndef clean_and_transform(df: pd.DataFrame, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Clean and transform raw DataFrame according to the expected schema.\n    Handles missing columns, type conversion, and basic data quality checks.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Add missing columns with default values\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col not in df.columns:\n            if col_type == bool:\n                df[col] = False\n            elif col_type == int:\n                df[col] = 0\n            elif col_type == 'date':\n                df[col] = pd.NaT\n            else:\n                df[col] = ''\n    \n    # Remove extra columns\n    df = df[list(expected_schema.keys())]\n    \n    # Type conversions and cleaning\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).fillna('')\n        elif col_type == int:\n            df[col] = pd.to_numeric(df[col], errors='coerce').fillna(0).astype(int)\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            # Accept various representations of boolean\n            df[col] = df[col].astype(str).str.strip().str.lower().map(\n                {'true': True, '1': True, 'yes': True, 'false': False, '0': False, 'no': False}\n            ).fillna(False)\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            df[col] = pd.to_datetime(df[col], errors='coerce')\n    \n    # Data quality checks\n    # Remove rows without customer_id or email\n    df = df[df['customer_id'].astype(str).str.strip() != '']\n    df = df[df['email'].astype(str).str.contains('@', na=False)]\n    df = df.drop_duplicates(subset=['customer_id'])\n    \n    # Fill missing names with 'Unknown'\n    df['first_name'] = df['first_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    df['last_name'] = df['last_name'].replace('', 'Unknown')\n    \n    # Ensure age is within reasonable bounds\n    df.loc[(df['age'] < 0) | (df['age'] > 120), 'age'] = 0\n    \n    # Fill missing signup_date with today's date\n    df['signup_date'] = df['signup_date'].fillna(pd.Timestamp.today().normalize())\n    \n    return df\n\n# -------------------- SCHEMA EVOLUTION HANDLING --------------------\n\ndef evolve_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Ensure the warehouse table matches the expected schema.\n    Adds missing columns as needed.\n    \"\"\"\n    cur = conn.cursor()\n    cur.execute(f\"PRAGMA table_info({table})\")\n    existing_cols = sql_type = 'DATE'\n            else:\n                sql_type = 'TEXT'\n            alter_sql = f\"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {col} {sql_type}\"\n            cur.execute(alter_sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\ndef create_table_if_not_exists(conn: sqlite3.Connection, table: str, expected_schema: Dict[str, Any]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Create the warehouse table if it does not exist.\n    \"\"\"\n    columns = []\n    for col, col_type in expected_schema.items():\n        if col_type == str:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        elif col_type == int:\n            sql_type = 'INTEGER'\n        elif col_type == bool:\n            sql_type = 'BOOLEAN'\n        elif col_type == 'date':\n            sql_type = 'DATE'\n        else:\n            sql_type = 'TEXT'\n        columns.append(f\"{col} {sql_type}\")\n    col_defs = ', '.join(columns)\n    sql = f\"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {table} ({col_defs}, PRIMARY KEY(customer_id))\"\n    conn.execute(sql)\n    conn.commit()\n\n# -------------------- LOAD TO DATA WAREHOUSE --------------------\n\ndef upsert_customers(conn: sqlite3.Connection, df: pd.DataFrame, table: str):\n    \"\"\"\n    Upsert (insert or replace) customer conn.cursor()\n    # Drop existing view if it exists\n    cur.execute(f\"DROP VIEW IF EXISTS {view_name}\")\n    # Create new view with derived columns and friendly names\n    cur.execute(f\"\"\"\n duplicate id\n                \"email\": \"test@example.com\",\n                \"age\": 200,  # invalid age\n                \"is_active\": \"True\"\n            }\n        ])\n        clean_df = clean_and_transform(df, self.expected_schema)\n        # Only one valid row should remain (c1, deduped, valid email)\n        self.assertEqual(len(clean_df), 1)\n        row = clean_df.iloc[0]\n        self.assertEqual(row['customer_id'], 'c1')\n        self.assertEqual(row['first_name'], 'Unknown')\n        self.assertEqual(row['last_name'], 'Unknown')\n        self.assertTrue(row['is_active'])\n        self.assertEqual(row['age'], 0)  # age > 120 set to 0\n        self.assertTrue('@' in row['email'])\n        self.assertIsInstance(row['signup_date'], pd.Timestamp)\n\n    def test_clean_and_transform_fill_missing_signup_date(self):\n        df = pd.DataFrame([{\n            \"customer_id\": \"c3\",\n            \"email\": \"foo@bar.com\",\n            \"first_name\": \"Foo\",\n            \"last_name\": \"Bar\",\n            \"country\": \"FR\",\n            \"age\": 20,\n            \"is_active\": True\n            # missing signup_date\n        }])\n        clean_df = clean_and_transform(df, self.expected_schema)\n        self.assertEqual(len(clean_df), 1)\n        row = clean_df.iloc[0]\n        today = pd.Timestamp.today().normalize()\n        self.assertEqual(row['signup_date'], today)\n\n    def test_schema_evolution(self):\n        # Create initial table with fewer columns\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)\n        conn.execute(\"CREATE TABLE customers (customer_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, email TEXT)\")\n        conn.commit()\n        # Evolve schema\n        evolve_schema(conn, self.table, self.expected_schema)\n        # Check columns\n        cur = conn.execute(\"PRAGMA table_info(customers)\")\n        columns = [row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()]\n        for col in self.expected_schema:\n            self.assertIn(col, columns)\n        conn.close()\n\n    def test_create_table_if_not_exists(self):\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)\n        create_table_if_not_exists(conn, self.table, self.expected_schema)\n        cur = conn.execute(\"PRAGMA table_info(customers)\")\n        columns = [row[1] for row in cur.fetchall()]\n        for col in self.expected_schema:\n            self.assertIn(col, columns)\n        conn.close()\n\n    def test_upsert_customers_and_load_to_warehouse(self):\n        df = pd.DataFrame([{\n            \"customer_id\": \"c1\",\n            \"first_name\": \"Alice\",\n            \"last_name\": \"Smith\",\n            \"email\": \"alice@example.com\",\n            \"signup_date\": pd.Timestamp(\"2022-01-01\"),\n            \"country\": \"US\",\n            \"age\": 30,\n            \"is_active\": True\n        }])\n        load_to_warehouse(df, self.db_path, self.table, self.expected_schema)\n        # Upsert with different data\n        df2 = pd.DataFrame([{\n            \"customer_id\": \"c1\",\n            \"first_name\": \"Alicia\",\n            \"last_name\": \"Smith\",\n            \"email\": \"alice@example.com\",\n            \"signup_date\": pd.Timestamp(\"2022-01-01\"),\n            \"country\": \"US\",\n            \"age\": 31,\n            \"is_active\": False\n        }])\n        load_to_warehouse(df2, self.db_path, self.table, self.expected_schema)\n        # Check in DB\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)\n        cur = conn.execute(\"SELECT first_name, age, is_active FROM customers WHERE customer_id='c1'\")\n        row = cur.fetchone()\n        self.assertEqual(row[0], 'Alicia')\n        self.assertEqual(row[1], 31)\n        # SQLite stores booleans as 0/1\n        self.assertIn(row[2], (0, 1, False, True))\n        conn.close()\n\n    def test_create_semantic_layer(self):\n        # Insert data\n        df = pd.DataFrame([\n            {\n                \"customer_id\": \"c1\",\n                \"first_name\": \"Alice\",\n                \"last_name\": \"Smith\",\n                \"email\": \"alice@example.com\",\n                \"signup_date\": pd.Timestamp(\"2000-01-01\"),\n                \"country\": \"US\",\n                \"age\": 17,\n                \"is_active\": True\n            },\n            {\n                \"customer_id\": \"c2\",\n                \"first_name\": \"Bob\",\n                \"last_name\": \"Brown\",\n                \"email\": \"bob@example.com\",\n                \"signup_date\": pd.Timestamp(\"1970-02-02\"),\n                \"country\": \"UK\",\n                \"age\": 65,\n                \"is_active\": False\n            }\n        ])\n        load_to_warehouse(df, self.db_path, self.table, self.expected_schema)\n        create_semantic_layer(self.db_path, self.table, self.view)\n        # Query the view\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)\n        cur = conn.execute(f\"SELECT id, full_name, age_group, signup_year FROM {self.view} ORDER BY id\")\n        rows = cur.fetchall()\n        self.assertEqual(len(rows), 2)\n        self.assertEqual(rows[0][0], 'c1')\n        self.assertEqual(rows[0][1], 'Alice Smith')\n        self.assertEqual(rows[0][2], 'Minor')\n        self.assertEqual(rows[0][3], '2000')\n        self.assertEqual(rows[1][2], 'Senior')\n        conn.close()\n\n    def test_pipeline_end_to_end(self):\n        # Write raw CSV and JSON\n        df_csv = pd.DataFrame([{\n            \"customer_id\": \"c10\",\n            \"first_name\": \"Jon\",\n            \"last_name\": \"Doe\",\n            \"email\": \"jon@example.com\",\n            \"signup_date\": \"2021-05-05\",\n            \"country\": \"US\",\n            \"age\": 25,\n            \"is_active\": True\n        }])\n        self.write_csv('raw1.csv', df_csv)\n        json_data = {\n            \"customer_id\": \"c11\",\n            \"first_name\": \"Jane\",\n            \"last_name\": \"Roe\",\n            \"email\": \"jane@example.com\",\n            \"signup_date\": \"2020-12-12\",\n            \"country\": \"CA\",\n            \"age\": 50,\n            \"is_active\": False\n        }\n        self.write_json('raw2.json', json_data)\n        # Run pipeline steps\n        raw_df = ingest_raw_files(self.test_dir)\n        clean_df = clean_and_transform(raw_df, self.expected_schema)\n        load_to_warehouse(clean_df, self.db_path, self.table, self.expected_schema)\n        create_semantic_layer(self.db_path, self.table, self.view)\n        # Check semantic view\n        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)\n        cur = conn.execute(f\"SELECT id, full_name, age, age_group FROM {self.view} ORDER BY id\")\n        rows = cur.fetchall()\n        self.assertEqual(len(rows), 2)\n        self.assertEqual(rows[0][0], 'c10')\n        self.assertEqual(rows[0][1], 'Jon Doe')\n        self.assertEqual(rows[0][3], 'Adult')\n        self.assertEqual(rows[1][0], 'c11')\n        self.assertEqual(rows[1][3], 'Adult')\n        conn.close()\n\n    def test_boolean_and_date_edge_cases(self):\n        # Various boolean representations, and date parsing\n        df = pd.DataFrame([\n            {\"customer_id\": \"b1\", \"email\": \"b1@e.com\", \"is_active\": \"1\", \"signup_date\": \"notadate\"},\n            {\"customer_id\": \"b2\", \"email\": \"b2@e.com\", \"is_active\": \"yes\", \"signup_date\": \"2020-01-01\"},\n            {\"customer_id\": \"b3\", \"email\": \"b3@e.com\", \"is_active\": \"false\", \"signup_date\": None},\n            {\"customer_id\": \"b4\", \"email\": \"b4@e.com\", \"is_active\": \"no\", \"signup_date\": \"\"},\n            {\"customer_id\": \"b5\", \"email\": \"b5@e.com\", \"is_active\": True, \"signup_date\": \"2022-02-02\"},\n            {\"customer_id\": \"b6\", \"email\": \"b6@e.com\", \"is_active\": False, \"signup_date\": \"2022-02-30\"},  # invalid date\n        ])\n        clean_df = clean_and_transform(df, self.expected_schema)\n        # All should be present\n        self.assertEqual(len(clean_df), 6)\n        # Check booleans\n        expected = [True, True, False, False, True, False]\n        self.assertListEqual(list(clean_df['is_active']), expected)\n        # Check dates: invalid dates should be filled with today\n        today = pd.Timestamp.today().normalize()\n        for i, sd in enumerate(clean_df['signup_date']):\n            if i in [0, 3, 5]:  # invalid or missing\n                self.assertEqual(sd, today)\n            elif i == 1:\n                self.assertEqual(sd, pd.Timestamp('2020-01-01'))\n            elif i == 4:\n                self.assertEqual(sd, pd.Timestamp('2022-02-02'))\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()",
